**Timestamp:** 2026-07-18T00:25:43.001Z

I’m using the GitHub workflow skill because this is repository-wide branch management with irreversible remote cleanup.

Each non-preview `TaleSession` is pinned to one published version and advances through idempotent, ordered events. The player receives its current projection and SSE updates; Captain actions call the same engine. Verification providers all enter through one versioned submission contract, so the simulator and a future paired helper cannot bypass progression rules. // @exec: {"max_output_tokens": 10000}
const abs = "C:\\Users\\kkids\\Documents\\Codex_TreasureHunt\\src\\components\\gm\\Quartermaster.tsx";
const chunks = [];
for (let skip = 0; skip < 1360; skip += 80) {
  const r = await tools.shell_command({
    command: `git show 'HEAD:src/components/gm/Quartermaster.tsx' | Select-Object -Skip ${skip} -First 80\nexit 0`,
    timeout_ms: 10000,
    workdir: "C:\\Users\\kkids\\Documents\\Codex_TreasureHunt"
  });
  const marker = "Output:\n";
  const part = r.slice(r.indexOf(marker) + marker.length).replace(/\r?\n$/, "");
  if (part.includes("truncated")) throw new Error(`Chunk ${skip} was truncated`);
  if (part.length) chunks.push(part);
}
const source = chunks.join("\n");
await tools.apply_patch(`*** Begin Patch\n*** Delete File: ${abs}\n*** End Patch`);
const added = source.split(/\r?\n/).map(line => `+${line}`).join("\n");
await tools.apply_patch(`*** Begin Patch\n*** Add File: ${abs}\n${added}\n*** End Patch`);
const patch = `*** Begin Patch\n*** Update File: ${abs}\n@@\n           {workspaces.map(([key, label, icon]) => (\n             <Link\n@@\n               <span>{label}</span>\n             </Link>\n           ))}\n+          <Link href=\"/studio\">\n+            <i aria-hidden=\"true\">S</i>\n+            <span>Tall Tale Studio</span>\n+          </Link>\n+          <Link href=\"/captain\">\n+            <i aria-hidden=\"true\">C</i>\n+            <span>Captain Sessions</span>\n+          </Link>\n         </nav>\n*** End Patch`;
await tools.apply_patch(patch);
text(`restored_lines=${source.split(/\r?\n/).length}`);
